info.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp,\n                            maxOffset, retainedRecords.size(), filteredBatchSize);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.RETAIN_EMPTY) {\n                if (batch.magic() < RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2) // should never happen\n                    throw new IllegalStateException(\"Empty batches are only supported for magic v2 and above\");\n\n                bufferOutputStream.ensureRemaining(DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n                DefaultRecordBatch.writeEmptyHeader(bufferOutputStream.buffer(), RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, batch.producerId(),\n                        batch.producerEpoch(), batch.baseSequence(), batch.baseOffset(), batch.lastOffset(),\n                        batch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), batch.timestampType(), batch.maxTimestamp(),\n                        batch.isTransactional(), batch.isControlBatch());\n                filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, 0, true);\n            }\n\n            // If we had to allocate a new buffer to fit the filtered buffer (see KAFKA-5316), return early to\n            // avoid the need for additional allocations.\n            ByteBuffer outputBuffer = bufferOutputStream.buffer();\n            if (outputBuffer != destinationBuffer) {\n                filterResult.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n                return filterResult;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return filterResult;\n    }\n\n    private static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\n                                                 BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\n                                                 FilterResult filterResult,\n                                                 RecordFilter filter) {\n        try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\n            long maxOffset = -1;\n            boolean containsTombstones = false;\n            // Convert records with old record versions\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iterator.next();\n                filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\n\n                if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\n                    if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\n                        maxOffset = record.offset();\n\n                    retainedRecords.add(record);\n\n                    if (!record.hasValue()) {\n                        containsTombstones = true;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    writeOriginalBatch = false;\n                }\n            }\n            return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class BatchFilterResult {\n        private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\n        private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\n        private final boolean containsTombstones;\n        private final long maxOffset;\n        private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                  final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\n                                  final boolean containsTombstones,\n                                  final long maxOffset) {\n            this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\n            this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\n            this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\n            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\n                                                                 List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                                                 ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\n                                                                 final long deleteHorizonMs) {\n        Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\n        // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\n        // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\n        // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\n        // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\n        TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\n        long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\n                originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\n                originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\n\n        // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\n        MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\n                compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\n                originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\n                originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\n\n        for (Record record : retainedRecords)\n            builder.append(record);\n\n        if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\n            // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\n            // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\n            // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\n            builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\n\n        return builder;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get a read-only duplicate view of the {@link ByteBuffer} that backs this instance.\n     *\n     * <p>The returned buffer shares the underlying byte array with this instance — no data is\n     * copied. Its position is reset to 0 and its limit reflects the full size of the records\n     * data. Modifications to the returned buffer's position and limit do not affect this instance,\n     * but mutations to the underlying bytes (e.g. via in-place {@link MutableRecordBatch} methods)\n     * will be visible through both the returned buffer and this instance.\n     *\n     * @return a duplicate of the backing {@link ByteBuffer} starting at position 0\n     */\n    public ByteBuffer buffer() {\n        return buffer.duplicate();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns a zero-copy {@link MemoryRecords} view over a sub-range of this instance's backing\n     * buffer. The slice shares the underlying bytes; no data is copied.\n     *\n     * <p>If {@code size} exceeds the number of bytes available from {@code position} to the end\n     * of the buffer, the slice is silently clamped to the available bytes.\n     *\n     * @param position the start position (0-based, inclusive) within this instance's buffer\n     * @param size     the desired number of bytes in the slice\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecords} backed by the specified sub-range\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if {@code position} is negative, {@code position} exceeds\n     *         the buffer limit, or {@code size} is negative\n     */\n    @Override\n    public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\n        if (position < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid position: \" + position + \" in read from \" + this);\n        if (position > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Slice from position \" + position + \" exceeds end position of \" + this);\n        if (size < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid size: \" + size + \" in read from \" + this);\n\n        int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\n        // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\n        // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\n        // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\n        // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\n        // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\n        // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\n        ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\n        slicedBuffer.position(position);\n        slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\n        // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\n        slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\n\n        return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns an {@link Iterable} over the {@link MutableRecordBatch} objects contained in this\n     * instance. The iterable is backed by a lazy {@link #batchIterator()} and can be iterated\n     * multiple times; each call to {@link Iterable#iterator()} creates a new independent iterator\n     * over the same underlying buffer.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> Batch-level metadata (offsets, timestamps, compression type) is\n     * read directly from the backing buffer without decompression. Record-level access requires\n     * explicit iteration into each batch.\n     *\n     * @return an {@link Iterable} of {@link MutableRecordBatch}; never {@code null}\n     */\n    @Override\n    public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\n        return batches;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"MemoryRecords(size=\" + sizeInBytes() +\n                \", buffer=\" + buffer +\n                \")\";\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        MemoryRecords that = (MemoryRecords) o;\n\n        return buffer.equals(that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer.hashCode();\n    }\n\n    public abstract static class RecordFilter {\n        public final long currentTime;\n        public final long deleteRetentionMs;\n\n        public RecordFilter(final long currentTime, final long deleteRetentionMs) {\n            this.currentTime = currentTime;\n            this.deleteRetentionMs = deleteRetentionMs;\n        }\n\n        public static class BatchRetentionResult {\n            public final BatchRetention batchRetention;\n            public final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            public BatchRetentionResult(final BatchRetention batchRetention,\n                                        final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) {\n                this.batchRetention = batchRetention;\n                this.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            }\n        }\n\n        public enum BatchRetention {\n            DELETE, // Delete the batch without inspecting records\n            RETAIN_EMPTY, // Retain the batch even if it is empty\n            DELETE_EMPTY  // Delete the batch if it is empty\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether the full batch can be discarded (i.e. whether we even need to\n         * check the records individually).\n         */\n        protected abstract BatchRetentionResult checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch batch);\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether a record should be retained in the log. Note that {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)}\n         * is used prior to checking individual record retention. Only records from batches which were not\n         * explicitly discarded with {@link BatchRetention#DELETE} will be considered.\n         */\n        protected abstract boolean shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch recordBatch, Record record);\n    }\n\n    public static class FilterResult {\n        private ByteBuffer outputBuffer;\n        private int messagesRead = 0;\n        // Note that `bytesRead` should contain only bytes from batches that have been processed, i.e. bytes from\n        // `messagesRead` and any discarded batches.\n        private int bytesRead = 0;\n        private int messagesRetained = 0;\n        private int bytesRetained = 0;\n        private long maxOffset = -1L;\n        private long maxTimestamp = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        private long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = -1L;\n\n        private FilterResult(ByteBuffer outputBuffer) {\n            this.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(MutableRecordBatch retainedBatch, int numMessagesInBatch, boolean headerOnly) {\n            int bytesRetained = headerOnly ? DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD : retainedBatch.sizeInBytes();\n            updateRetainedBatchMetadata(retainedBatch.maxTimestamp(), retainedBatch.lastOffset(),\n                    retainedBatch.lastOffset(), numMessagesInBatch, bytesRetained);\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset,\n                                                 int messagesRetained, int bytesRetained) {\n            validateBatchMetadata(maxTimestamp, shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, maxOffset);\n            if (maxTimestamp > this.maxTimestamp) {\n                this.maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp;\n                this.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n            }\n            this.maxOffset = Math.max(maxOffset, this.maxOffset);\n            this.messagesRetained += messagesRetained;\n            this.bytesRetained += bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        private void validateBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset) {\n            if (maxTimestamp != RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP && shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"shallowOffset undefined for maximum timestamp \" + maxTimestamp);\n            if (maxOffset < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"maxOffset undefined\");\n        }\n\n        public ByteBuffer outputBuffer() {\n            return outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        public int messagesRead() {\n            return messagesRead;\n        }\n\n        public int bytesRead() {\n            return bytesRead;\n        }\n\n        public int messagesRetained() {\n            return messagesRetained;\n        }\n\n        public int bytesRetained() {\n            return bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        public long maxOffset() {\n            return maxOffset;\n        }\n\n        public long maxTimestamp() {\n            return maxTimestamp;\n        }\n\n        public long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n            return shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a read-only {@link MemoryRecords} view over the given {@link ByteBuffer}. The\n     * buffer's current position is treated as the start of the first batch; the limit determines\n     * the total readable size.\n     *\n     * <p>No data is copied — the returned instance shares the underlying byte array with the\n     * supplied buffer.\n     *\n     * @param buffer the buffer containing encoded record batches; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return a {@link MemoryRecords} backed by {@code buffer}\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords readableRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        return new MemoryRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for constructing a new batch using the current magic\n     * version, the given compression and timestamp type, and starting at {@code baseOffset}.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type ({@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME} or\n     *                      {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME})\n     * @param baseOffset    the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for constructing a new batch using the current magic\n     * version, the given compression and timestamp type, starting at {@code baseOffset}, and\n     * capped at {@code maxSize} bytes.\n     *\n     * <p>When the timestamp type is {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}, the log-append\n     * timestamp is set to the current wall-clock time at the moment this method is called.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset    the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @param maxSize       maximum number of bytes the builder may write into {@code buffer}\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               int maxSize) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n\n        return new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n            logAppendTime, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE,\n            false, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH, maxSize);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for constructing a new batch with the specified\n     * magic version, compression, timestamp type, and explicit log-append time. No idempotent or\n     * transactional producer metadata is set.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param magic         the record format magic byte\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset    the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @param logAppendTime the log-append timestamp to embed in the batch header;\n     *                      use {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} if not applicable\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with the specified magic version, compression, and\n     * timestamp type. The log-append timestamp is set automatically if the timestamp type is\n     * {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}. No idempotent or transactional producer metadata is\n     * set.\n     *\n     * @param buffer        the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param magic         the record format magic byte\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset    the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with the specified magic version, compression,\n     * timestamp type, log-append time, and partition leader epoch. No idempotent or transactional\n     * producer metadata is set.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param magic                the record format magic byte\n     * @param compression          the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param timestampType        the timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset           the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @param logAppendTime        the log-append timestamp;\n     *                             use {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP} if not applicable\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the partition leader epoch to embed in the batch header\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} for building a transactional or idempotent batch\n     * using the current magic version and {@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME}. The producer\n     * identity ({@code producerId}, {@code producerEpoch}, {@code baseSequence}) and the\n     * transactional flag are embedded in the batch header.\n     *\n     * @param buffer          the buffer to write the encoded batch into; must not be {@code null}\n     * @param compression     the compression codec to apply to record data\n     * @param baseOffset      the base offset of the first record in the batch\n     * @param producerId      the idempotent/transactional producer id\n     * @param producerEpoch   the producer epoch\n     * @param baseSequence    the base sequence number for duplicate detection\n     * @param isTransactional {@code true} if the batch is part of an ongoing transaction\n     * @return a new {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} ready to accept records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence,\n                                               boolean isTransactional) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, baseOffset,\n                RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with the given magic version, compression, timestamp\n     * type, log-append time, and full idempotent producer metadata.                int baseSequence,\n                                               boolean isTransactional,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return /**\n     * Creates a {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} with full control over all batch header fields,\n     * including the control-batch flag.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               the buffer to Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                          int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n                logAppendTime, producerId, given {@link SimpleRecord} objects using the\n     * specified magic version, compression, initial offset, and\n     * {@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME}.\n     *\n     * @param magic         the It is the fundamental unit of data transfer between producers,\n * brokers, and consumers.\n *\n * <p>The batch format has evolved over three major versions, identified by the {@link #magic()} byte:\n * <ul>\n *   <li><b>Magic v0</b> ({@link #MAGIC_VALUE_V0}): Legacy format. A batch always contains exactly\n *       one record when uncompressed; multiple records are allowed only under compression.</li>\n *   <li><b>Magic v1</b> ({@link #MAGIC_VALUE_V1}): Adds per-record timestamps. Same single-record\n *       constraint as v0 when uncompressed.</li>\n *   <li><b>Magic v2</b> ({@link #MAGIC_VALUE_V2}) and above: Current format. Batches generally\n *       contain multiple records regardless of compression. Adds idempotent producer support\n *       (producer id, epoch, sequence numbers) and transactional semantics.</li>\n * </ul>\n *\n * <p>Instances of this interface are obtained by iterating over a {@link Records} object (e.g.\n * {@link MemoryRecords} or {@code FileRecords}) via {@link Records#batches()}. They provide\n * shallow access to batch-level metadata (offsets, timestamps, producer identity, compression) as\n * well as deep access to the individual {@link Record} objects contained within.\n *\n * <p><b>Thread-safety:</b> Implementations of this interface are <em>not</em> thread-safe.\n * External synchronisation is required when a single batch instance is accessed concurrently from\n * multiple threads. In practice, batches are short-lived objects consumed on a single thread\n * during fetch or log-append operations.\n *\n * @see MemoryRecords\n * @see DefaultRecordBatch\n * @see Record\n */\npublic interface RecordBatch extends Iterable<Record> {\n\n    /**\n     * The \"magic\" values\n     */\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V0 = 0;\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V1 = 1;\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V2 = 2;\n\n    /**\n     * The current \"magic\" value\n     */\n    byte CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE = MAGIC_VALUE_V2;\n\n    /**\n     * Timestamp value for records without a timestamp\n     */\n    long NO_TIMESTAMP = -1L;\n\n    /**\n     * Values used in the v2 record format by non-idempotent/non-transactional producers or when\n     * up-converting from an older format.\n     */\n    long NO_PRODUCER_ID = -1L;\n    short NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH = -1;\n    int NO_SEQUENCE = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Used to indicate an unknown leader epoch, which will be the case when the record set is\n     * first created by the producer.\n     */\n    int NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether the checksum of this batch is correct.\n     *\n     * @return true If so, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isValid();\n\n    /**\n     * Raise an exception if the checksum is not valid.\n     *\n     * @throws org.apache.kafka.common.errors.CorruptRecordException if the batch checksum does not\n     *         match the recomputed value, indicating data corruption\n     */\n    void ensureValid();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the checksum of this record batch, which covers the batch header as well as all of the records.\n     *\n     * @return The 4-byte unsigned checksum represented as a long\n     */\n    long checksum();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the max timestamp or log append time of this record batch.\n     *\n     * If the timestamp type is create time, this is the max timestamp among all records contained in this batch and\n     * the value is updated during compaction.\n     *\n     * @return The max timestamp\n     */\n    long maxTimestamp();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the timestamp type of this record batch. This will be {@link TimestampType#NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE}\n     * if the batch has magic 0.\n     *\n     * @return The timestamp type\n     */\n    TimestampType timestampType();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the base offset contained in this record batch. For magic version prior to 2, the base offset will\n     * always be the offset of the first message in the batch. This generally requires deep iteration and will\n     * return the offset of the first record in the record batch. For magic version 2 and above, this will return\n     * the first offset of the original record batch (i.e. prior to compaction). For non-compacted topics, the\n     * behavior is equivalent.\n     *\n     * Because this requires deep iteration for older magic versions, this method should be used with\n     * caution. Generally {@link #lastOffset()} is safer since access is efficient for all magic versions.\n     *\n     * @return The base offset of this record batch (which may or may not be the offset of the first record\n     *         as described above).\n     */\n    long baseOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the last offset in this record batch (inclusive). Just like {@link #baseOffset()}, the last offset\n     * always reflects the offset of the last record in the original batch, even if it is removed during log\n     * compaction.\n     *\n     * @return The offset of the last record in this batch\n     */\n    long lastOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the offset following this record batch (i.e. the last offset contained in this batch plus one).\n     *\n     * @return the next consecutive offset following this batch\n     */\n    long nextOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the record format version of this record batch (i.e its magic value).\n     *\n     * @return the magic byte\n     */\n    byte magic();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the producer id for this log record batch. For older magic versions, this will return -1.\n     *\n     * @return The producer id or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    long producerId();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the producer epoch for this log record batch.\n     *\n     * @return The producer epoch, or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    short producerEpoch();\n\n    /**\n     * Does the batch have a valid producer id set.\n     *\n     * @return {@code true} if the producer id is set (i.e. not {@link #NO_PRODUCER_ID}),\n     *         {@code false} otherwise\n     */\n    boolean hasProducerId();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the base sequence number of this record batch. Like {@link #baseOffset()}, this value is not\n     * affected by compaction: it always retains the base sequence number from the original batch.\n     *\n     * @return The first sequence number or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    int baseSequence();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the last sequence number of this record batch. Like {@link #lastOffset()}, the last sequence number\n     * always reflects the sequence number of the last record in the original batch, even if it is removed during log\n     * compaction.\n     *\n     * @return The last sequence number or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    int lastSequence();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the compression type of this record batch.\n     *\n     * @return The compression type\n     */\n    CompressionType compressionType();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the size in bytes of this batch, including the size of the record and the batch overhead.\n     * @return The size in bytes of this batch\n     */\n    int sizeInBytes();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the count if it is efficiently supported by the record format (which is only the case\n     * for magic 2 and higher).\n     *\n     * @return The number of records in the batch or null for magic versions 0 and 1.\n     */\n    Integer countOrNull();\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether this record batch is compressed.\n     * @return true if so, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isCompressed();\n\n    /**\n     * Write this record batch into a buffer.\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write the batch to\n     */\n    void writeTo(ByteBuffer buffer);\n\n    /**\n     * Whether or not this record batch is part of a transaction.\n     * @return true if it is, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isTransactional();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the delete horizon, returns OptionalLong.EMPTY if the first timestamp is not the delete horizon\n     * @return timestamp of the delete horizon\n     */\n    OptionalLong deleteHorizonMs();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the partition leader epoch of this record batch.\n     * @return The leader epoch or -1 if it is unknown\n     */\n    int partitionLeaderEpoch();\n\n    /**\n     * Return a streaming iterator which basically delays decompression of the record stream until the records\n     * are actually asked for using {@link Iterator#next()}. If the message format does not support streaming\n     * iteration, then the normal iterator is returned. Either way, callers should ensure that the iterator is closed.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> For compressed batches, this iterator decompresses records lazily on demand,\n     * avoiding the need to allocate memory for all decompressed records up-front. Reusing the\n     * {@link BufferSupplier}-supplied buffers across calls (e.g. via a thread-local pool) can\n     * significantly reduce GC pressure, especially for large batches or high-throughput consumers.\n     *\n     * @param decompressionBufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if supported.\n     *                                    For small record batches, allocating a potentially large buffer (64 KB for LZ4)\n     *                                    will dominate the cost of decompressing and iterating over the records in the\n     *                                    batch. As such, a supplier that reuses buffers will have a significant\n     *                                    performance impact.\n     * @return The closeable iterator\n     */\n    CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier);\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether this is a control batch (i.e. whether the control bit is set in the batch attributes).\n     * For magic versions prior to 2, this is always false.\n     *\n     * @return Whether this is a batch containing control records\n     */\n    boolean isControlBatch();\n\n    /**\n     * Iterate all records to find the offset of the record with the maximum timestamp.\n     *\n     * <p>Notes:\n     * <ol>\n     *   <li>If multiple records share the same maximum timestamp, the offset of the earliest such\n     *       record is returned.</li>\n     *   <li>Always returns {@link Optional#empty()} when {@link #magic()} equals\n     *       {@link #MAGIC_VALUE_V0}, because v0 batches carry no per-record timestamps.</li>\n     * </ol>\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> This default implementation performs a full scan of all records\n     * via {@link #streamingIterator(BufferSupplier)}, including decompression for compressed\n     * batches. Avoid calling this method in hot paths unless necessary.\n     *\n     * @return the offset of the record with the maximum timestamp, or {@link Optional#empty()} for\n     *         magic v0 batches or when no matching record is found\n     */\n    default Optional<Long> offsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n        if (magic() == RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V0) return Optional.empty();\n        long maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iter = streamingIterator(BufferSupplier.create())) {\n            while (iter.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iter.next();\n                if (maxTimestamp == record.timestamp()) return Optional.of(record.offset());\n            }\n        }\n        return Optional.empty();\n    }\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":374,"cache_read_input_tokens":86746,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":374,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"2ca7ce3c-8dc4-4f9d-9e5f-7961fd2c27a9","uuid":"746a4b81-ca15-4496-ad27-df5c49bb81a4"}

{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-sonnet-4-6","id":"msg_01Vc2XMmknUEWp2WQt9tS8Zs","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01RYsFDHaFaFRnY3LA9Y5T5V","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/record/internal/DefaultRecordBatch.java","content":"/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one or more\n * contributor license agreements. This class provides both read and\n * in-place-mutation access to a single batch encoded in the Kafka binary wire format. The on-wire\n * schema is:\n *\n * <pre>\n * RecordBatch =&gt;\n *   BaseOffset            =&gt; Int64\n *   Length                =&gt; Int32\n *   PartitionLeaderEpoch  =&gt; Int32\n *   Magic                 =&gt; Int8\n *   CRC                   =&gt; Uint32\n *   Attributes            =&gt; Int16\n *   LastOffsetDelta       =&gt; Int32  // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\n *   BaseTimestamp         =&gt; Int64\n *   MaxTimestamp          =&gt; Int64\n *   ProducerId            =&gt; Int64\n *   ProducerEpoch         =&gt; Int16\n *   BaseSequence          =&gt; Int32\n *   RecordsCount          =&gt; Int32\n *   Records               =&gt; [Record]\n * </pre>\n *\n * <p>When compression is enabled (see attributes below), the compressed record data is serialized\n * directly following the count of the number of records.\n *\n * <p>The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that\n * follow the CRC). It is located after the magic byte, which means that clients must parse the\n * magic byte before deciding how to interpret the bytes between the batch length and the magic\n * byte. The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC computation to avoid the need\n * to recompute the CRC when this field is assigned for every batch that is received by the broker.\n * The CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial is used for the computation.\n *\n * <p><b>Compaction:</b> Unlike the older message formats, magic v2 and above preserves the first\n * and last offset/sequence numbers from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is\n * required in order to be able to restore the producer's state when the log is reloaded. If we did\n * not retain the last sequence number, then following a partition leader failure, once the new\n * leader has rebuilt the producer state from the log, the next sequence expected number would no\n * longer be in sync with what was written by the client. This would cause an unexpected\n * {@code OutOfOrderSequence} error, which is typically fatal. The base sequence number must be\n * preserved for duplicate checking: the broker checks incoming Produce requests for duplicates by\n * verifying that the first and last sequence numbers of the incoming batch match the last from that\n * producer.\n *\n * <p>Note that if all of the records in a batch are removed during compaction, the broker may\n * still retain an empty batch header in order to preserve the producer sequence information as\n * described above. These empty batches are retained only until either a new sequence number is\n * written by the corresponding producer or the producerId is expired from lack of activity.\n *\n * <p>There is no similar need to preserve the timestamp from the original batch after compaction.\n * The {@code BaseTimestamp} field therefore reflects the timestamp of the first record in the\n * batch in most cases. If the batch is empty, the {@code BaseTimestamp} will be set to\n * {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP}. If the delete horizon flag is set to 1, the\n * {@code BaseTimestamp} will be set to the time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction\n * markers in the batch should be removed.\n *\n * <p>Similarly, the {@code MaxTimestamp} field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current\n * records if the timestamp type is {@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME}. For\n * {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}, on the other hand, the {@code MaxTimestamp} field\n * reflects the timestamp set by the broker and is preserved after compaction. Additionally, the\n * {@code MaxTimestamp} of an empty batch always retains the previous value prior to becoming empty.\n *\n * <p>The current attributes bit layout:\n * <pre>\n *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  | Unused (7-15) | Delete Horizon Flag (6) | Control (5) | Transactional (4) | Timestamp Type (3) | Compression Type (0-2) |\n *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * </pre>\n *\n * <p><b>Thread-safety:</b> This class is <em>not</em> thread-safe. The underlying\n * {@link ByteBuffer} is accessed without synchronisation. Concurrent reads or any combination of\n * reads and in-place mutations (e.g. {@link #setLastOffset}, {@link #setMaxTimestamp},\n * {@link #setPartitionLeaderEpoch}) from multiple threads requires external synchronisation.\n *\n * @see RecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecords\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder\n */\npublic class DefaultRecordBatch extends AbstractRecordBatch implements MutableRecordBatch {\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET = 0;\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int LENGTH_OFFSET = BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET + BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH;\n    static final int      return buffer.get(MAGIC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void ensureValid() {\n        if (sizeInBytes() < RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD)\n            throw new      int baseSequence = baseSequence();\n        if (baseSequence == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\n            return RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE;\n        return incrementSequence(baseSequence, @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBufferOutputStream outputStream) {\n        outputStream.write(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isTransactional() {\n  }\n            };\n        } else {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long            }\n            };\n        }\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> uncompressedIterator() {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n This class provides both read and\n * in-place-mutation access to a single batch encoded in the Kafka binary wire format. The on-wire\n * schema is:\n *\n * <pre>\n * RecordBatch =&gt;\n *   BaseOffset            =&gt; Int64\n *   Length                =&gt; Int32\n *   PartitionLeaderEpoch  =&gt; Int32\n *   Magic                 =&gt; Int8\n *   CRC                   =&gt; Uint32\n *   Attributes            =&gt; Int16\n *   LastOffsetDelta       =&gt; Int32  // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\n *   BaseTimestamp         =&gt; Int64\n *   MaxTimestamp          =&gt; Int64\n *   ProducerId            =&gt; Int64\n *   ProducerEpoch         =&gt; Int16\n *   BaseSequence          =&gt; Int32\n *   RecordsCount          =&gt; Int32\n *   Records               =&gt; [Record]\n * </pre>\n *\n * <p>When compression is enabled (see attributes below), the compressed record data is serialized\n * directly following the count of the number of records.\n *\n * <p>The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that\n * follow the CRC). It is located after the magic byte, which means that clients must parse the\n * magic byte before deciding how to interpret the bytes between the batch length and the magic\n * byte. The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC computation to avoid the need\n * to recompute the CRC when this field is assigned for every batch that is received by the broker.\n * The CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial is used for the computation.\n *\n * <p><b>Compaction:</b> Unlike the older message formats, magic v2 and above preserves the first\n * and last offset/sequence numbers from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is\n * required in order to be able to restore the producer's state when the log is reloaded. If we did\n * not retain the last sequence number, then following a partition leader failure, once the new\n * leader has rebuilt the producer state from the log, the next sequence expected number would no\n * longer be in sync with what was written by the client. This would cause an unexpected\n * {@code OutOfOrderSequence} error, which is typically fatal. The base sequence number must be\n * preserved for duplicate checking: the broker checks incoming Produce requests for duplicates by\n * verifying that the first and last sequence numbers of the incoming batch match the last from that\n * producer.\n *\n * <p>Note that if all of the records in a batch are removed during compaction, the broker may\n * still retain an empty batch header in order to preserve the producer sequence information as\n * described above. These empty batches are retained only until either a new sequence number is\n * written by the corresponding producer or the producerId is expired from lack of activity.\n *\n * <p>There is no similar need to preserve the timestamp from the original batch after compaction.\n * The {@code BaseTimestamp} field therefore reflects the timestamp of the first record in the\n * batch in most cases. If the batch is empty, the {@code BaseTimestamp} will be set to\n * {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP}. If the delete horizon flag is set to 1, the\n * {@code BaseTimestamp} will be set to the time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction\n * markers in the batch should be removed.\n *\n * <p>Similarly, the {@code MaxTimestamp} field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current\n * records if the timestamp type is {@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME}. For\n * {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}, on the other hand, the {@code MaxTimestamp} field\n * reflects the timestamp set by the broker and is preserved after compaction. Additionally, the\n * {@code MaxTimestamp} of an empty batch always retains the previous value prior to becoming empty.\n *\n * <p>The current attributes bit layout:\n * <pre>\n *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  | Unused (7-15) | Delete Horizon Flag (6) | Control (5) | Transactional (4) | Timestamp Type (3) | Compression Type (0-2) |\n *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * </pre>\n *\n * <p><b>Thread-safety:</b> This class is <em>not</em> thread-safe. The underlying\n * {@link ByteBuffer} is accessed without synchronisation. Concurrent reads or any combination of\n * reads and in-place mutations (e.g. {@link #setLastOffset}, {@link #setMaxTimestamp},\n * {@link #setPartitionLeaderEpoch}) from multiple threads requires external synchronisation.\n *\n * @see RecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecords\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder\n */\npublic class DefaultRecordBatch extends AbstractRecordBatch implements MutableRecordBatch    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterator<Record> iterator() {\n        if (count() == 0)\n            return Collections.emptyIterator();\n\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // for a normal iterator, we cannot ensure that the underlying compression stream is closed,\n        // so we decompress the full record set here. Use cases which call for a lower memory footprint\n        // can use `streamingIterator` at the cost of additional complexity\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = compressedIterator(BufferSupplier.NO_CACHING, false)) {\n            List<Record> records = new ArrayList<>(count());\n            while (iterator.hasNext())\n                records.add(iterator.next());\n            return records.iterator();\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> skipKeyValueIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (count() == 0) {\n            return CloseableIterator.wrap(Collections.emptyIterator());\n        }\n\n        /*\n         * For uncompressed iterator, it is actually not worth skipping key / value / headers at all since\n         * its ByteBufferInputStream's skip() function is less efficient compared with just reading it actually\n         * as it will allocate new byte array.\n         */\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // we define this to be a closable iterator so that caller (i.e. the log validator) needs to close it\n        // while we can save memory footprint of not decompressing the full record set ahead of time\n        return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, true);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (isCompressed())\n            return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, false);\n        else\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setLastOffset(long offset) {\n        buffer.putLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, offset - lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType timestampType, long maxTimestamp) {\n        long currentMaxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        // We don't need to recompute crc if the timestamp is not updated.\n        if (timestampType() == timestampType && currentMaxTimestamp == maxTimestamp)\n            return;\n\n        byte attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType(), timestampType, isTransactional(), isControlBatch(), hasDeleteHorizonMs());\n        buffer.putShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        long crc = computeChecksum();\n        ByteUtils.writeUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET, crc);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int epoch) {\n        buffer.putInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long checksum() {\n        return ByteUtils.readUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    public boolean isValid() {\n        return sizeInBytes() >= RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD && checksum() == computeChecksum();\n    }\n\n    private long computeChecksum() {\n        return Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, buffer.limit() - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private byte attributes() {\n        // note we're not using the second byte of attributes\n        return (byte) buffer.getShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        DefaultRecordBatch that = (DefaultRecordBatch) o;\n        return Objects.equals(buffer, that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer != null ? buffer.hashCode() : 0;\n    }\n\n    private static byte computeAttributes(CompressionType type, TimestampType timestampType,\n                                          boolean isTransactional, boolean isControl, boolean isDeleteHorizonSet) {\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timestamp type must be provided to compute attributes for message \" +\n                    \"format v2 and above\");\n\n        byte attributes = isTransactional ? TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK : 0;\n        if (isControl)\n            attributes |= CONTROL_FLAG_MASK;\n        if (type.id > 0)\n            attributes |= (byte) (COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK & type.id);\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            attributes |= TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK;\n        if (isDeleteHorizonSet)\n            attributes |= DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK;\n        return attributes;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Writes an empty (zero-record) batch header into the given buffer at its current position.\n     * This is used during log compaction to preserve producer sequence metadata when all records\n     * in a batch have been deleted.\n     *\n     * <p>The written header occupies exactly {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes. The CRC is\n     * computed and written as part of this call.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               the destination buffer; must have at least\n     *                             {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes remaining\n     * @param magic                the record format magic byte; must be\n     *                             {@link RecordBatch#MAGIC_VALUE_V2} or higher\n number to embed in the header\n     * @param baseOffset           the base (first) offset of the original batch\n     * @param lastOffset           the last offset of the original batch\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the leader epoch at the time the batch was written\n     * @param timestampType        the timestamp type ({@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME} or\n     *                             {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME})\n     * @param timestamp            the timestamp to record in the header\n     * @param isTransactional      whether this batch was produced as part of a transaction\n     * @param isControlRecord      whether this batch is a control batch\n     * @see #writeHeader\n     */\n    public static void writeEmptyHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                        byte magic,\n                                        long producerId,\n                                        short producerEpoch,\n                                        int baseSequence,\n                                        long baseOffset,\n                                        long lastOffset,\n                                        int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                        TimestampType timestampType,\n                                        long timestamp,\n                                        boolean isTransactional,\n                                        boolean isControlRecord) {\n        int offsetDelta = (int) (lastOffset - baseOffset);\n        writeHeader(buffer, baseOffset, offsetDelta, DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD, magic,\n                    CompressionType.NONE, timestampType, RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP, timestamp, producerId,\n                    producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, isControlRecord, false, partitionLeaderEpoch, 0);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Encodes a complete magic v2 batch header into the given buffer at its current position and\n     * advances the buffer position by {@link #RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD} bytes. The CRC-32C checksum\n     * covering all header fields from the attributes to the end of the declared batch size is\n     * computed and written inline.\n     *\n     * <p>This is a low-level method used by {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} during batch\n     * serialisation. Most callers should use {@link MemoryRecords#builder} or\n     * {@link #writeEmptyHeader} instead.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               the destination buffer; must have at least {@code sizeInBytes}\n     *                             bytes remaining from the current position\n     * @param baseOffset           the base (first) offset of the batch\n     * @param lastOffsetDelta      difference between the last and base offsets in the batch\n     * @param sizeInBytes          total serialised size of the batch in bytes, including this header\n     * @param magic                the record format magic byte; must be\n     *                             {@link RecordBatch#MAGIC_VALUE_V2} or higher\n     * @param compressionType      the compression codec used for the record data\n isDeleteHorizonSet   whether the delete horizon flag should be set in the attributes;\n     *                             when true, {@code baseTimestamp} encodes the delete horizon time\n     * magic} is below\n     *         {@link RecordBatch#CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE} or if {@code baseTimestamp} is negative and\n     *         not equal to {@link RecordBatch#NO_TIMESTAMP}\n     */\n    public static void writeHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                   long baseOffset,\n                                   int lastOffsetDelta,\n                                   int sizeInBytes,\n                                   byte magic,\n                                   CompressionType compressionType,\n                                   TimestampType timestampType,\n                                   long baseTimestamp,\n                                   long maxTimestamp,\n                                   long producerId,\n                                   short epoch,\n                                   int sequence,\n                                   boolean isTransactional,\n                                   boolean isControlBatch,\n                                   boolean isDeleteHorizonSet,\n                                   int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                   int numRecords) {\n        if (magic < RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid magic value \" + magic);\n        if (baseTimestamp < 0 && baseTimestamp != NO_TIMESTAMP)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid message timestamp \" + baseTimestamp);\n\n        short attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType, timestampType, isTransactional, isControlBatch, isDeleteHorizonSet);\n\n        int position = buffer.position();\n        buffer.putLong(position + BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, baseOffset);\n        buffer.putInt(position + LENGTH_OFFSET, sizeInBytes - LOG_OVERHEAD);\n        buffer.putInt(position + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n        buffer.put(position + MAGIC_OFFSET, magic);\n        buffer.putShort(position + ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(position + BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, baseTimestamp);\n        buffer.putLong(position + MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        buffer.putInt(position + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET, lastOffsetDelta);\n        buffer.putLong(position + PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET, producerId);\n        buffer.putShort(position + PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n        buffer.putInt(position + BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET, sequence);\n        buffer.putInt(position + RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET, numRecords);\n        long crc = Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, sizeInBytes - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n        buffer.putInt(position + CRC_OFFSET, (int) crc);\n        buffer.position(position + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n all records in order to accumulate\n     * per-record sizes (including variable-length fields and varint-encoded deltas). It does not\n     * account for the overhead of any compression codec.\n     *\n     * @param baseOffset the base offset of the batch; used to compute per-record offset deltas\n     * @param records    the records whose encoded sizes should be summed; must not be {@code null}\n     * @return the total batch size in bytes (header plus all record bytes), or {@code 0} if\n     *         {@code records} is empty\n     */\n    public static int sizeInBytes(long baseOffset, Iterable<Record> records) {\n        Iterator<Record> iterator = records.iterator();\n        if (!iterator.hasNext())\n            return 0;\n\n        int size = RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD;\n        Long baseTimestamp = null;\n        while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n            Record record = iterator.next();\n            int offsetDelta = (int) (record.offset() - baseOffset);\n            if (baseTimestamp == null)\n                baseTimestamp = record.timestamp();\n            long timestampDelta = record.timestamp() - baseTimestamp;\n            size += DefaultRecord.sizeInBytes(offsetDelta, timestampDelta, record.key(), record.value(),\n                    record.headers());\n        }\n        return size;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Computes the serialised size in bytes of a magic v2 batch containing the given\n     * {@link SimpleRecord} objects, assuming sequential offset assignment starting at delta 0.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> This method iterates over all records in order to accumulate\n     * per-record sizes. It does not account for the overhead of any compression codec.\n     *\n     * @param records the simple records whose encoded sizes should be summed; must not be\n     *                {@code null}\n     * @return the total batch size in bytes (header plus all record bytes), or {@code 0} if\n     *         {@code records} is empty\n     */\n    public static int sizeInBytes(Iterable<SimpleRecord> records) {\n        Iterator<SimpleRecord> iterator = records.iterator();\n        if (!iterator.hasNext())\n            return 0;\n\n        int size = RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD;\n        int offsetDelta = 0;\n        Long baseTimestamp = null;\n        while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n            SimpleRecord record = iterator.next();\n            if (baseTimestamp == null)\n                baseTimestamp = record.timestamp();\n            long timestampDelta = record.timestamp() - baseTimestamp;\n            size += DefaultRecord.sizeInBytes(offsetDelta++, timestampDelta, record.key(), record.value(),\n                    record.headers());\n        }\n        return size;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get an upper bound on the size of a batch with only a single record using a given key and value. This\n     * is only an estimate because it does not take into account additional overhead from the compression\n     * algorithm used.\n     */\n    static int estimateBatchSizeUpperBound(ByteBuffer key, ByteBuffer value, Header[] headers) {\n        return RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + DefaultRecord.recordSizeUpperBound(key, value, headers);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Increments a producer sequence number by {@code increment}, wrapping around at\n     * {@link Integer#MAX_VALUE} according to the Kafka sequence-number arithmetic.\n     *\n     * <p>Kafka sequence numbers are unsigned 31-bit integers that wrap around modulo\n     * {@code Integer.MAX_VALUE + 1}. This method implements the wrap-around correctly so that\n     * brokers can detect duplicate and out-of-order produce requests even across sequence-number\n     * rollovers.\n     *\n     * @param sequence  the current base sequence number; must be non-negative\n     * @param increment the value to add; must be non-negative\n     * @return the resulting sequence number after incrementing, with wrap-around applied\n     * @see #decrementSequence(int, int)\n     */\n    public static int incrementSequence(int sequence, int increment) {\n        if (sequence > Integer.MAX_VALUE - increment)\n            return increment - (Integer.MAX_VALUE - sequence) - 1;\n        return sequence + increment;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Decrements a producer sequence number by {@code decrement}, wrapping around at zero\n     * according to the Kafka sequence-number arithmetic.\n     *\n     * <p>This is the inverse of {@link #incrementSequence(int, int)}. decrementSequence(int sequence, int decrement) {\n        if (sequence < decrement)\n            return Integer.MAX_VALUE - (decrement - sequence) + 1;\n        return sequence - decrement;\n    }\n\n    // visible for testing\n    abstract class RecordIterator implements CloseableIterator<Record> {\n        private final Long logAppendTime;\n        private final long baseOffset;\n        private
