The timestamp type is {@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME}.\n     *\n     * @param initialOffset        the base offset to assign to the first record\n     * @param compression          the compression codec to apply\n     * @param producerId           the transactional producer id\n     * @param producerEpoch        the producer epoch\n     * @param baseSequence         the base sequence number\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the partition leader epoch\n     * @param records              the records to include; varargs\n     * @return an immutable {@link MemoryRecords} containing the serialised transactional batch\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withTransactionalRecords(long initialOffset, Compression compression, long producerId,\n                                                         short producerEpoch, int baseSequence, int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                                         SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withTransactionalRecords(RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, initialOffset, compression,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, partitionLeaderEpoch, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds a {@link MemoryRecords} containing the given {@link SimpleRecord} objects using the\n     * specified magic version, initial offset, compression, and timestamp type. No idempotent or\n     * transactional metadata is embedded.\n     *\n     * @param magic         the record format magic byte\n     * @param initialOffset the base offset to assign to the first record\n     * @param compression   the compression codec to apply\n     * @param timestampType the timestamp type\n     * @param records       the records to include; varargs\n     * @return an immutable {@link MemoryRecords} containing the serialised batch\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(byte magic, long initialOffset, Compression compression,\n                                            TimestampType timestampType, SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withRecords(magic, initialOffset, compression, timestampType, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH,\n                false, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds a {@link MemoryRecords} containing the given {@link SimpleRecord} objects with full\n     * control over all batch header fields. This is the most general {@code withRecords} overload;\n     * all other overloads delegate to this method.\n     *\n     * <p><b>Performance note:</b> The method estimates the required buffer size upfront based on\n     * {@link AbstractRecords#estimateSizeInBytes} and uses a resizable\n     * {@link ByteBufferOutputStream} to handle cases where the estimate is too small. Only a\n     * single batch is created per call.\n     *\n     * @param magic                the record format magic byte\n     * @param initialOffset        the base offset to assign to the first record\n     * @param compression          the compression codec to apply\n     * @param timestampType        the timestamp type\n     * @param producerId           the idempotent/transactional producer id, or\n     *                             {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_ID}\n     * @param producerEpoch        the producer epoch, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH}\n     * @param baseSequence         the base sequence number, or {@link RecordBatch#NO_SEQUENCE}\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the partition leader epoch\n     * @param isTransactional      {@code true} if the batch belongs to a transaction\n     * @param records              the records to include; varargs\n     * @return an immutable {@link MemoryRecords} containing the serialised batch, or\n     *         {@link #EMPTY} if {@code records} is empty\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(byte magic, long initialOffset, Compression compression,\n                                            TimestampType timestampType, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                            int baseSequence, int partitionLeaderEpoch, boolean isTransactional,\n                                            SimpleRecord... records) {\n        if (records.length == 0)\n            return MemoryRecords.EMPTY;\n        int sizeEstimate = AbstractRecords.estimateSizeInBytes(magic, compression.type(), Arrays.asList(records));\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(sizeEstimate);\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferStream, magic, compression, timestampType,\n                initialOffset, logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, false,\n                partitionLeaderEpoch, sizeEstimate)) {\n            for (SimpleRecord record : records)\n                builder.append(record);\n            return builder.build();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds a {@link MemoryRecords} containing a single end-of-transaction control batch for the\n     * given producer, using offset 0 and the current wall-clock time as the timestamp.\n     *\n     * @param producerId    the transactional producer id\n     * @param producerEpoch the producer epoch\n     * @param marker        the {@link EndTransactionMarker} describing the transaction outcome\n     * @return an immutable {@link MemoryRecords} containing the end-transaction control batch\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long producerId, short producerEpoch, EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        return withEndTransactionMarker(0L, System.currentTimeMillis(), RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, marker);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds a {@link MemoryRecords} containing a single end-of-transaction control batch for the\n     * given producer, using offset 0 and the specified timestamp.\n     *\n     * @param timestamp     the timestamp to embed in the batch header (milliseconds since epoch)\n     * @param producerId    the transactional producer id\n     * @param producerEpoch the producer epoch\n     * @param marker        the {@link EndTransactionMarker} describing the transaction outcome\n     * @return an immutable {@link MemoryRecords} containing the end-transaction control batch\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long timestamp, long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                         EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        return withEndTransactionMarker(0L, timestamp, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH, producerId,\n                producerEpoch, marker);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds a {@link MemoryRecords} containing a single end-of-transaction control batch with\n     * the given initial offset, timestamp, partition leader epoch, and producer identity.\n     *\n     * @param initialOffset        the base offset to assign to the control batch\n     * @param timestamp            the timestamp to embed in the batch header (milliseconds since epoch)\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch the partition leader epoch\n     * @param producerId           the transactional producer id\n     * @param producerEpoch        the producer epoch\n     * @param marker               the {@link EndTransactionMarker} describing the transaction outcome\n     * @return an immutable {@link MemoryRecords} containing the end-transaction control batch\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withEndTransactionMarker(long initialOffset, long timestamp, int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                                         long producerId, short producerEpoch,\n                                                         EndTransactionMarker marker) {\n        int endTxnMarkerBatchSize = DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + marker.endTxnMarkerValueSize();\n        ByteBuffer buffer = ByteBuffer.allocate(endTxnMarkerBatchSize);\n        writeEndTransactionalMarker(buffer, initialOffset, timestamp, partitionLeaderEpoch, producerId,\n                producerEpoch, marker);\n        buffer.flip();\n        return MemoryRecords.readableRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Encodes a single end-of-transaction control batch directly into the given {@link EndTransactionMarker)} for\n     * callers that already manage their own buffer.\n     *\n     * @param buffer               the destination buffer; must have sufficient remaining capacity\n     *     the {@link EndTransactionMarker} describing the transaction outcome\n     */\n    public static void writeEndTransactionalMarker(ByteBuffer buffer, long initialOffset, long timestamp,\n TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, initialOffset, timestamp, producerId, producerEpoch,\n                RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, isTransactional, true, partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                buffer.capacity())\n        ) {\n            builder.appendEndTxnMarker(timestamp, marker);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Builds a {@link MemoryRecords} containing a single KRaft control batch
